# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/cilium--v1.16.5`
- Use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/cilium--v1.16.5$` filter in keyword_search
- Use `github.com/sg-evals/cilium--v1.16.5` as the `repo` parameter for go_to_definition/find_references/read_file


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

**Sourcegraph Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/cilium--v1.16.5`

# Task: Implement PolicyAuditLogger for Cilium

## Objective
Create a `PolicyAuditLogger` in `pkg/policy/` that provides structured logging of policy
evaluation decisions for audit and debugging purposes.

## Requirements

1. **Create `pkg/policy/audit_logger.go`** with:
   - `PolicyAuditLogger` struct with configurable log level and output
   - `LogDecision(identity, policy, verdict, reason)` method
   - `LogEvaluation(ctx, policyKey, selectorCache, result)` method
   - Integration with Cilium's existing logging framework (logrus/scopedLog)
   - Support for JSON-structured audit log output

2. **Create `pkg/policy/audit_logger_test.go`** with tests

3. **Follow Cilium patterns**:
   - Use `logfields` package for structured log fields
   - Follow the `SelectorCache` interaction pattern
   - Use `lock.Mutex` from `pkg/lock/` for thread safety

## Key Reference Files
- `pkg/policy/distillery.go` — policy decision evaluation
- `pkg/policy/selectorcache.go` — SelectorCache for identity matching
- `pkg/policy/types.go` — policy types and interfaces
- `pkg/logging/logfields/logfields.go` — structured log field constants
- `pkg/lock/lock.go` — Cilium's lock primitives

## Success Criteria
- PolicyAuditLogger struct and methods exist
- Uses Cilium's logging framework (logrus/scopedLog)
- Has LogDecision method with policy verdict logging
- Thread-safe implementation
- Test file exists with test functions

=== audit_logger.go Overview ===
// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0
// Copyright Authors of Cilium

package policy

import (
	"context"
	"io"
	"os"

	"github.com/sirupsen/logrus"

	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/identity"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/lock"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/logging/logfields"
)

// PolicyAuditLogger provides structured logging of policy evaluation decisions
// for audit and debugging purposes.
type PolicyAuditLogger struct {
	lock.Mutex
	logger   *logrus.Logger
	logLevel logrus.Level
}

// PolicyDecision represents the result of a policy evaluation
type PolicyDecision int

const (
	PolicyDecisionAllow PolicyDecision = iota
	PolicyDecisionDeny
)

// String returns the string representation of a policy decision
func (pd PolicyDecision) String() string {
	switch pd {
	case PolicyDecisionAllow:
		return "ALLOW"
	case PolicyDecisionDeny:
		return "DENY"
	default:
		return "UNKNOWN"
	}
}

// NewPolicyAuditLogger creates a new PolicyAuditLogger with the specified log level and output.
// If output is nil, logs are written to os.Stderr.
func NewPolicyAuditLogger(level logrus.Level, output io.Writer) *PolicyAuditLogger {
	logger := logrus.New()
	logger.SetLevel(level)

	// Set output
	if output == nil {
		output = os.Stderr
	}
	logger.SetOutput(output)

	// Configure JSON formatting for structured audit logs
	logger.SetFormatter(&logrus.JSONFormatter{})

...

func TestLogDecision(t *testing.T) {

- **PolicyDecision enum**: Type-safe representation of allow/deny verdicts

  - `NewPolicyAuditLogger(level, output)` - Creates logger with JSON formatting
  - `LogDecision(identity, policy, verdict, reason)` - Logs policy verdicts
  - `LogEvaluation(ctx, policyKey, selectorCache, result)` - Logs evaluations
  - `SetLogLevel()/GetLogLevel()` - Dynamic log level control

- All methods protected with `lock.Mutex`

{
  "content": "// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0\n// Copyright Authors of Cilium\n\npackage policy\n\nimport (\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"io\"\n\t\"os\"\n\n\t\"github.com/sirupsen/logrus\"\n\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/identity\"\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/lock\"\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/logging/logfields\"\n)\n\n// PolicyAuditLogger provides structured logging of policy evaluation decisions\n// for audit and debugging purposes.\ntype PolicyAuditLogger struct {\n\tlock.Mutex\n\tlogger   *logrus.Logger\n\tlogLevel logrus.Level\n}\n\n// PolicyDecision represents the result of a policy evaluation\ntype PolicyDecision int\n\nconst (\n\tPolicyDecisionAllow PolicyDecision = iota\n\tPolicyDecisionDeny\n)\n\n// String returns the string representation of a policy decision\nfunc (pd PolicyDecision) String() string {\n\tswitch pd {\n\tcase PolicyDecisionAllow:\n\t\treturn \"ALLOW\"\n\tcase PolicyDecisionDeny:\n\t\treturn \"DENY\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"UNKNOWN\"\n\t}\n}\n\n// NewPolicyAuditLogger creates a new PolicyAuditLogger with the specified log level and output.\n// If output is nil, logs are written to os.Stderr.\nfunc NewPolicyAuditLogger(level logrus.Level, output io.Writer) *PolicyAuditLogger {\n\tlogger := logrus.New()\n\tlogger.SetLevel(level)\n\n\t// Set output\n\tif output == nil {\n\t\toutput = os.Stderr\n\t}\n\tlogger.SetOutput(output)\n\n\t// Configure JSON formatting for structured audit logs\n\tlogger.SetFormatter(&logrus.JSONFormatter{})\n\n\treturn &PolicyAuditLogger{\n\t\tlogger:   logger,\n\t\tlogLevel: level,\n\t}\n}\n\n// LogDecision logs a policy decision with identity, policy, verdict, and reason.\n// This method is thread-safe.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogDecision(\n\tidentity *identity.Identity,\n\tpolicy interface{},\n\tverdict PolicyDecision,\n\treason string,\n) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\tif !pal.logger.IsLevelEnabled(pal.logLevel) {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tfields := logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.Identity: identity.ID,\n\t\t\"decision\":         verdict.String(),\n\t\tlogfields.Reason:   reason,\n\t}\n\n\tif policy != nil {\n\t\tfields[\"policy\"] = policy\n\t}\n\n\tscopedLog := pal.logger.WithFields(fields)\n\tscopedLog.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\t\"event\": \"policy_decision\",\n\t}).Info(\"Policy decision logged\")\n}\n\n// LogEvaluation logs a policy evaluation with context, policy key, selector cache, and result.\n// This method is thread-safe.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogEvaluation(\n\tctx context.Context,\n\tpolicyKey interface{},\n\tselectorCache (\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"io\"\n\t\"os\"\n\n\t\"github.com/sirupsen/logrus\"\n\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/identity\"\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/lock\"\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/logging/logfields\"\n)\n\n// PolicyAuditLogger provides structured logging of policy evaluation decisions\n// for audit and debugging purposes.\ntype PolicyAuditLogger struct {\n\tlock.Mutex\n\tlogger   *logrus.Logger\n\tlogLevel logrus.Level\n}\n\n// PolicyDecision represents the result of a policy evaluation\ntype PolicyDecision int\n\nconst (\n\tPolicyDecisionAllow PolicyDecision = iota\n\tPolicyDecisionDeny\n)\n\n// String returns the string representation of a policy decision\nfunc (pd PolicyDecision) String() string {\n\tswitch pd {\n\tcase PolicyDecisionAllow:\n\t\treturn \"ALLOW\"\n\tcase PolicyDecisionDeny:\n\t\treturn \"DENY\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"UNKNOWN\"\n\t}\n}\n\n// NewPolicyAuditLogger creates a new PolicyAuditLogger with the specified log level and output.\n// If output is nil, logs are written to os.Stderr.\nfunc NewPolicyAuditLogger(level logrus.Level, output io.Writer) *PolicyAuditLogger {\n\tlogger := logrus.New()\n\tlogger.SetLevel(level)\n\n\t// Set output\n\tif output == nil {\n\t\toutput = os.Stderr\n\t}\n\tlogger.SetOutput(output)\n\n\t// Configure JSON formatting for structured audit logs\n\tlogger.SetFormatter(&logrus.JSONFormatter{})\n\n\treturn &PolicyAuditLogger{\n\t\tlogger:   logger,\n\t\tlogLevel: level,\n\t}\n}\n\n// LogDecision logs a policy decision with identity, policy, verdict, and reason.\n// This method is thread-safe.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogDecision(\n\tidentity *identity.Identity,\n\tpolicy interface{},\n\tverdict PolicyDecision,\n\treason identity.ID,\n\t\t\"decision\":         verdict.String(),\n\t\tlogfields.Reason:   reason,\n\t}\n\n\tif policy != nil {\n\t\tfields[\"policy\"] = policy\n\t}\n\n\tscopedLog := pal.logger.WithFields(fields)\n\tscopedLog.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\t\"event\": \"policy_decision\",\n\t}).Info(\"Policy decision logged\")\n}\n\n// LogEvaluation logs a policy evaluation with context, policy key, selector cache, and result.\n// This method is thread-safe.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogEvaluation(\n\tctx context.Context,\n\tpolicyKey interface{},\n\tselectorCache *SelectorCache,\n\tresult interface{},\n) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\tif !pal.logger.IsLevelEnabled(pal.logLevel) {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tfields := logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.PolicyKey: policyKey,\n\t\t\"event\":             \"policy_evaluation\",\n\t}\n\n\tif selectorCache != nil {\n\t\tfields[\"cache_info\"] = \"selectorCache_present\"\n\t}\n\n\tif result != nil {\n\t\tfields[\"result\"] = result\n\t}\n\n\tscopedLog := pal.logger.WithFields(fields)\n\tscopedLog.Info(\"Policy evaluation logged\")\n}\n\n// SetLogLevel sets the log level for the audit logger\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) SetLogLevel(level logrus.Level) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\tpal.logLevel = pal.logLevel\n}\n",

PolicyAuditLogger provides structured logging of policy evaluation decisions\n// for audit and debugging purposes.\ntype PolicyAuditLogger struct {\n\tlock.Mutex\n\tlogger   *logrus.Logger\n\tlogLevel logrus.Level\n}\n\n// PolicyDecision represents the result of a policy evaluation\ntype PolicyDecision int\n\nconst (\n\tPolicyDecisionAllow PolicyDecision = iota\n\tPolicyDecisionDeny\n)\n\n// String returns the string representation of a policy decision\nfunc (pd PolicyDecision) String() string {\n\tswitch pd {\n\tcase PolicyDecisionAllow:\n\t\treturn \"ALLOW\"\n\tcase PolicyDecisionDeny:\n\t\treturn \"DENY\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"UNKNOWN\"\n\t}\n}\n\n// NewPolicyAuditLogger creates a new PolicyAuditLogger with the specified log level and output.\n// If output is nil, logs are written to os.Stderr.\nfunc NewPolicyAuditLogger(level logrus.Level, output io.Writer) *PolicyAuditLogger {\n\tlogger := logrus.New()\n\tlogger.SetLevel(level)\n\n\t// Set output\n\tif output == nil {\n\t\toutput = os.Stderr\n\t}\n\tlogger.SetOutput(output)\n\n\t// Configure JSON formatting for structured audit logs\n\tlogger.SetFormatter(&logrus.JSONFormatter{})\n\n\treturn &PolicyAuditLogger{\n\t\tlogger:   logger,\n\t\tlogLevel: level,\n\t}\n}\n\n// LogDecision logs a policy decision with identity, policy, verdict, and reason.\n// This method is thread-safe.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogDecision(\n\tidentity *identity.Identity,\n\tpolicy interface{},\n\tverdict PolicyDecision,\n\treason string,\n) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\tif !pal.logger.IsLevelEnabled(pal.logLevel) {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tfields := logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.Identity: identity.ID,\n\t\t\"decision\":         verdict.String(),\n\t\tlogfields.Reason:   reason,\n\t}\n\n\tif policy != nil {\n\t\tfields[\"policy\"] = policy\n\t}\n\n\tscopedLog := pal.logger.WithFields(fields)\n\tscopedLog.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\t\"event\": \"policy_decision\",\n\t}).Info(\"Policy decision logged\")\n}\n\n// LogEvaluation logs a policy evaluation with context, policy key, selector cache, and result.\n// This method is thread-safe.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogEvaluation(\n\tctx context.Context,\n\tpolicyKey interface{},\n\tselectorCache *SelectorCache,\n\tresult interface{},\n) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\tif !pal.logger.IsLevelEnabled(pal.logLevel) {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tfields := logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.PolicyKey: policyKey,\n\t\t\"event\":             \"policy_evaluation\",\n\t}\n\n\tif selectorCache != nil {\n\t\tfields[\"cache_info\"] = \"selectorCache_present\"\n\t}\n\n\tif result != nil {\n\t\tfields[\"result\"] = result\n\t}\n\n\tscopedLog := pal.logger.WithFields(fields)\n\tscopedLog.Info(\"Policy evaluation logged\")\n}\n\n// SetLogLevel sets the log level for the audit logger\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) SetLogLevel(level logrus.Level) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\tpal.logLevel = level\n\tpal.logger.SetLevel(level)\n}\n\n// GetLogLevel returns the current log level\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) GetLogLevel() logrus.Level {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\treturn pal.logLevel\n}\n",

1. WRITE /workspace/pkg/policy/audit_logger.go
// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0
// Copyright Authors of Cilium

package policy

import (
	"context"
	"io"
	"os"

	"github.com/sirupsen/logrus"

	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/identity"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/lock"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/logging/logfields"
)

// PolicyAuditLogger provides structured logging of policy evaluation decisions
// for audit and debugging purposes.
type PolicyAuditLogger struct {
	lock.Mutex
	logger   *logrus.Logger
	logLevel logrus.Level
}

// PolicyDecision represents the result of a policy evaluation
type PolicyDecision int

const (
	PolicyDecisionAllow PolicyDecision = iota
	PolicyDecisionDeny
)

// String returns the string representation of a policy decision
func (pd PolicyDecision) String() string {
	switch pd {
	case PolicyDecisionAllow:
		return "ALLOW"
	case PolicyDecisionDeny:
		return "DENY"
	default:
		return "UNKNOWN"
	}
}

// NewPolicyAuditLogger creates a new PolicyAuditLogger with the specified log level and output.
// If output is nil, logs are written to os.Stderr.
func NewPolicyAuditLogger(level logrus.Level, output io.Writer) *PolicyAuditLogger {
	logger := logrus.New()
	logger.SetLevel(level)

	// Set output
	if output == nil {
		output = os.Stderr
	}
	logger.SetOutput(output)

	// Configure JSON formatting for structured audit logs
	logger.SetFormatter(&logrus.JSONFormatter{})

	return &PolicyAuditLogger{
		logger:   logger,
		logLevel: level,
	}
}

// LogDecision logs a policy decision with identity, policy, verdict, and reason.
// This method is thread-safe.
func (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogDecision(
	identity *identity.Identity,
	policy interface{},
	verdict PolicyDecision,
	reason string,
) {
	pal.Lock()
	defer pal.Unlock()

	if !pal.logger.IsLevelEnabled(pal.logLevel) {
		return
	}

	fields := l
... (truncated)

// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0
// Copyright Authors of Cilium

package policy

import (
	"bytes"
	"context"
	"encoding/json"
	"testing"

	"github.com/sirupsen/logrus"
	"github.com/stretchr/testify/require"

	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/identity"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/labels"
)

func TestPolicyAuditLoggerCreation(t *testing.T) {
	buffer := &bytes.Buffer{}
	logger := NewPolicyAuditLogger(logrus.InfoLevel, buffer)
	require.NotNil(t, logger)
	require.Equal(t, logrus.InfoLevel, logger.GetLogLevel())
}

func TestPolicyAuditLoggerCreationWithNilOutput(t *testing.T) {
	logger := NewPolicyAuditLogger(logrus.InfoLevel, nil)
	require.NotNil(t, logger)
	require.Equal(t, logrus.InfoLevel, logger.GetLogLevel())
}

func TestLogDecision(t *testing.T) {
	buffer := &bytes.Buffer{}
	logger := NewPolicyAuditLogger(logrus.InfoLevel, buffer)

	// Create a test identity
	identityLabels := labels.ParseLabelArray("app=web")
	testIdentity := identity.Identity{
		ID:     identity.NumericIdentity(1001),
		Labels: identityLabels,
	}

	// Log a decision
	logger.LogDecision(&testIdentity, "test-policy", PolicyDecisionAllow, "security rule matched")

	// Verify output
	output := buffer.String()
	require.NotEmpty(t, output)
	require.Contains(t, output, "policy_decision")
	require.Contains(t, output, "ALLOW")
	require.Contains(t, output, "security rule matched")

	// Verify JSON format
	var logEntry map[string]interface{}
	err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(output), &logEntry)
	require.NoError(t, err)
	require.Equal(t, float64(1001), logEntry[logfields.Identity])
}

Implements the `PolicyAuditLogger` struct with the following components:

#### Types

2. **LogDecision(identity *identity.Identity, policy interface{}, verdict PolicyDecision, reason string)**

   - Uses `logfields.Identity` and `logfields.Reason`

3. **LogEvaluation(ctx context.Context, policyKey interface{}, selectorCache *SelectorCache, result interface{})**
   - Logs policy evaluations with context
   - Thread-safe implementation
   - Uses `logfields.PolicyKey`

   - Dynamic log level control
   - Thread-safe getters/setters
